`js/src/jit/`:\\n\\n### 1. Top-Level Ion Compiler Orchestration\\n**File:** `js/src/jit/Ion.cpp` (repo: github.com/sg-evals/firefox--871325b8)\\n**Key Symbol:** `IonCompile()` (static function at line 1765)\\n\\nThe `IonCompile` function is the main entry point for the Ion optimizing compiler. It:\\n- Allocates and initializes compilation state (TempAllocator, MIRGraph, CompileInfo, MIRGenerator)\\n- Creates a WarpSnapshot for the compilation\\n- Either schedules off-thread compilation via `IonCompileTask` or performs synchronous back-end compilation\\n- Manages linking of compiled code\\n\\n### 2. Off-Thread Compilation Task\\n**Header:** `js/src/jit/IonCompileTask.h` (repo: github.com/sg-evals/firefox--871325b8)\\n**Source:** `js/src/jit/IonCompileTask.cpp` (repo: github.com/sg-evals/firefox--871325b8)\\n**Key Class:** `IonCompileTask` (line 27 in header)\\n\\nThe `IonCompileTask` class represents a single off-thread Ion compilation task. It:\\n- Inherits from `HelperThreadTask` and `mozilla::LinkedListElement<IonCompileTask>`\\n- Holds the MIRGenerator and optional CodeGenerator (backgroundCodegen_)\\n- Implements `runTask()` to compile the backend on helper threads\\n- Implements `runHelperThreadTask()` to integrate results back on the main thread\\n\\n### 3. First-Tier JIT Compiler (Baseline)\\n**Header:** `js/src/jit/BaselineJIT.h` (repo: github.com/sg-evals/firefox--871325b8)\\n**Source:** `js/src/jit/BaselineJIT.cpp` (repo: github.com/sg-evals/firefox--871325b8)\\n**Key Class:** `BaselineScript` (line 189 in header)\\n\\nThe `BaselineScript` class represents the compiled output of the Baseline JIT compiler (first-tier, faster to compile). It:\\n- Uses trailing array layout for memory efficiency (resumeEntryList, retAddrEntries, osrEntries, debugTrapEntries)\\n- Stores the compiled JitCode method pointer and pending Ion compilation tasks\\n- Provides OSR (On-Stack Replacement) entries for transitioning to Ion code\\n- Manages debug instrumentation and profiler toggles\\n\\n### 4. Per-Runtime JIT State\\n**Header:** `js/src/jit/JitRuntime.h` (repo: github.com/sg-evals/firefox--871325b8)\\n**Key Class:** `JitRuntime` (defined in header)\\n\\nThe `JitRuntime` class manages per-runtime JIT compilation state:\\n- Maintains BaselineICFallbackCode for IC stubs\\n- Tracks IonCompileTask lists (ionLazyLinkList_)\\n- Manages off-thread compilation task batches\\n- Stores pre-generated trampoline code for VM functions\\n- Integrates Ion compilation tasks for lazy linking on the main thread\\n\\n### 5. JIT Configuration Options\\n**Header:** `js/src/jit/JitOptions.h` (repo: github.com/sg-evals/firefox--871325b8)\\n**Source:** `js/src/jit/JitOptions.cpp` (repo: github.com/sg-evals/firefox--871325b8)\\n**Key Class/Struct:** `DefaultJitOptions` (line 46 in header)\\n\\nThe `DefaultJitOptions` struct (exposed as global `JitOptions`) controls JIT configuration:\\n- Baseline interpreter and JIT thresholds (baselineInterpreterWarmUpThreshold, baselineJitWarmUpThreshold)\\n- Ion compilation thresholds (normalIonWarmUpThreshold)\\n- Optimization passes (inlining, GVN, range analysis, scalar replacement, etc.)\\n- Register allocator selection\\n- Spectre mitigation flags\\n- Debug and profiling options\\n\\n### Compilation Pipeline Flow\\n\\n1. **Entry:** Script execution triggers `IonCompile()` in Ion.cpp when warm-up thresholds are met\\n2. **Preparation:** MIRGenerator and graph are created with optimization info from JitOptions\\n3. **Off-Thread Decision:** If `options.offThreadCompilationAvailable()`, create IonCompileTask and schedule on helper thread\\n4. **Back-End Compilation:** Call `CompileBackEnd()` which generates machine code from MIR\\n5. **Linking:** Call `LinkCodeGen()` to finalize the IonScript and integrate with JitRuntime\\n6. **Fallback:** BaselineScript serves as first-tier JIT for faster
